CREATE TABLE comptes (
  Idcompte NUMBER(10,0) primary key,
  NCompte varchar2(25),
  Solde float ,
  NoClient NUMBER,
  CodeAgence NUMBER);
alter table comptes add CONSTRAINT f1 FOREIGN key( NoClient)
 REFERENCES  Client( NoClient) on DELETE  CASCADE ;
alter table comptes add CONSTRAINT f2 FOREIGN key( CODEAGENCE)
 REFERENCES  AGENCE( CODEAGENCE) on DELETE  CASCADE ;
